	  lib/selexonFunctions2.py: * Changed how we do sinedon queries for
	  all appion files!!!
	  * Deleted all references to apDB, leginondb, appiondb and clean
	  up query and insert styles.
	  * Libraries were all tested to make sure they import
	  * Bin folder files were all tested to make sure they import and
	  print help messages
	  
	  examples:
	  > fscq = appionData.ApFSCData()
	  
	  old direct query version:
	  > appiondb.direct_query(appionData.ApFSCData, 14)
	  new direct query version:
	  > appionData.ApFSCData.direct_query(14)
	  
	  old queryversion:
	  > appiondb.query(fscq, results=1)
	  new query version:
	  > fscq.query(results=1)
	  
	  old insert version:
	  > appiondb.insert(fscq)
	  new insert version:
	  > fscq.insert()

2006-08-05  Gabe Lander

	* [r25] particle_manager/makestack.py: made the "inspection" option
	  functional. User must specify a text file that
	  contains the output of the "imageassessor" node in leginon.
	  Eventually this data should be placed in the database, and this
	  information
	  read from there, not a text file.
	* [r24] particle_manager/selexon.py: - cleaned up the output to the
	  shell:
	  - downsample & filter now only output "downsizing and filtering
	  image"
	  - peakfinder now only writes out how many peaks have been found
	  - if using the crudfinder, tells user how many particles were
	  removed
	  - if crudfinder removes all the peaks, selexon will inform user
	  of this and go to
	  the next image. Selexon was crashing before in this case.
	  - moved placement of call to write logfile for the "continue"
	  option to the end,
	  in the case that an error occurred during the processing of an
	  image after finding peaks.

	* [r9] particle_manager/selexon.py: - changed jpg from crud
	  detection to be created in the same manner as
	  in the "createJPG" function
	  image is scaled down by half iteratively until desired binning is
	  reached
	* [r8] particle_manager/selexon.py: - fixed error in selexon loop:
	  if no particles are found in an image and the user has specified
	  to
	  either create box files or run the crud finder, these will be
	  skipped
	  and the next image will be processed.
	* [r7] particle_manager/selexon.py: - Added 3 more "crud" options:
	  crudblur - blur amount for edge detection
	  crudhi & crudlo - upper and lower thresholds for edge detection
	  If not entered on the command line, the default values are set.
	  
	  - Updated the help documentation to include these
	  
	  - Fixed the "crudonly" option so that it works with wild cards
	  now
	  
	  - Parameter parser now checks that if "crud" or "crudonly"
	  directly
	  follow the file name on the input, that these are not files.
